Clinical Recommendations:

Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Above optimal homocysteine - high homocysteine can be a risk factor for heart disease. Yours is not high but optimal levels are around 8. Levels can be reduced by supplementing with a good vitamin B complex or a "homocysteine lowering formula" like the one from solal.

Overview Notes: Above optimal homocysteine - high homocysteine can be a risk factor for heart disease. Yours is not high but optimal levels are around 8. Levels can be reduced by supplementing with a good vitamin B complex or a "homocysteine lowering formula" like the one from solal.
Comment Key: WomensHealthNote
